Semdegi faqtobrivi garemoebebi: Sps `apolinas~ sawesdebo kapitali


Seadgens 1428 aSS dolaris ekvivalent lars da sawesdebo kapitalis


Sevseba unda ganxorcielebuliyo arafuladi qonebrivi Senatanis


saxiT. sawarmos registraciis masalebSi, aseve, Sps-s wesdebaSi (5.2


muxlSi), ar aris miTiTebuli, Tu ra obieqtia Setanili sawesdebo


kapitalSi uZravi qonebis saxiT; ar aris miTiTebuli, vin ra qoneba


Seitana. aRniSnulidan gamomdinare, saapelacio sasamarTlom miiCnia,

mier ar aris ganxorcielebuli. sasamarTlom ganCinebis samarTlebriv


safuZvlad miuTiTa `mewarmeTa Sesaxeb~ kanonis 3.3, 5.4 da 5.8 muxlebze.

gauqmebas im safuZvliT, rom sasamarTlom sazogadoebis (Sps-s) valde-


bulebaze pasuxi mosTxova mis partniorebs. kerZod, sarCeli Setanili


iyo Sps-s mimarT, sasamarTlom ki mopasuxeebad miiwvia partniorebi da


ara warmomadgenlobiTi uflebamosilebiT aRWurvili piri.


kasatorebs miaCniaT, rom isini (partniorebi) mocemul saqmeSi


arasaTanado mopasuxeebi arian.

sarCelis safuZvlebs da Tavisi iniciativiT miuTiTa registraciis


gauqmebis damatebiT safuZvlebze, roca ganCinebaSi aRniSna, rom sawes-


debo kapitalis qonebrivi Senatanis Setanis Sesaxeb miTiTebuli unda


iyos registraciis maslebSi (wesdebaSi). aRniSnuliT sasamarTlom


Secvala gasaCivrebuli gadawyvetilebis motivacia, rac kasatorebs


saproceso normis (sssk-is 390-e muxlis) darRvevad miaCniaT, radgan

arsebiTad ar wydeba, miiReba ganCinebis formiT. am SemTxvevaSi ki


sasamarTlom saqmis arsebiT mxarezec imsjela.
